My Business Lodging API . locations

Instance Methods

lodging()

Returns the lodging Resource.

close()

Close httplib2 connections.

getLodging(name, readMask=None, x__xgafv=None)

Returns the Lodging of a specific location.

updateLodging(name, body=None, updateMask=None, x__xgafv=None)

Updates the Lodging of a specific location.

Method Details

close() 
Close httplib2 connections.
getLodging(name, readMask=None, x__xgafv=None) 
Returns the Lodging of a specific location.

Args:
  name: string, Required. Google identifier for this location in the form: `locations/{location_id}/lodging` (required)
  readMask: string, Required. The specific fields to return. Use "*" to include all fields. Repeated field items cannot be individually specified.
  x__xgafv: string, V1 error format.
    Allowed values
      1 - v1 error format
      2 - v2 error format

Returns:
  An object of the form:

    { # Lodging of a location that provides accomodations.
  "accessibility": { # Physical adaptations made to the property in consideration of varying levels of human physical ability. # Physical adaptations made to the property in consideration of varying levels of human physical ability.
    "mobilityAccessible": True or False, # Mobility accessible. Throughout the property there are physical adaptations to ease the stay of a person in a wheelchair, such as auto-opening doors, wide elevators, wide bathrooms or ramps.
    "mobilityAccessibleElevator": True or False, # Mobility accessible elevator. A lift that transports people from one level to another and is built to accommodate a wheelchair-using passenger owing to the width of its doors and placement of call buttons.
    "mobilityAccessibleElevatorException": "A String", # Mobility accessible elevator exception.
    "mobilityAccessibleException": "A String", # Mobility accessible exception.
    "mobilityAccessibleParking": True or False, # Mobility accessible parking. The presence of a marked, designated area of prescribed size in which only registered, labeled vehicles transporting a person with physical challenges may park.
    "mobilityAccessibleParkingException": "A String", # Mobility accessible parking exception.
    "mobilityAccessiblePool": True or False, # Mobility accessible pool. A swimming pool equipped with a mechanical chair that can be lowered and raised for the purpose of moving physically challenged guests into and out of the pool. May be powered by electricity or water. Also known as pool lift.
    "mobilityAccessiblePoolException": "A String", # Mobility accessible pool exception.
  },
  "activities": { # Amenities and features related to leisure and play. # Amenities and features related to leisure and play.
    "beachAccess": True or False, # Beach access. The hotel property is in close proximity to a beach and offers a way to get to that beach. This can include a route to the beach such as stairs down if hotel is on a bluff, or a short trail. Not the same as beachfront (with beach access, the hotel's proximity is close to but not right on the beach).
    "beachAccessException": "A String", # Beach access exception.
    "beachFront": True or False, # Breach front. The hotel property is physically located on the beach alongside an ocean, sea, gulf, or bay. It is not on a lake, river, stream, or pond. The hotel is not separated from the beach by a public road allowing vehicular, pedestrian, or bicycle traffic.
    "beachFrontException": "A String", # Beach front exception.
    "bicycleRental": True or False, # Bicycle rental. The hotel owns bicycles that it permits guests to borrow and use. Can be free or for a fee.
    "bicycleRentalException": "A String", # Bicycle rental exception.

    "boutiqueStoresException": "A String", # Boutique stores exception.

    "nightclub": True or False, # Nightclub. There is a room at the hotel with a bar, a dance floor, and seating where designated staffers play dance music. There may also be a designated area for the performance of live music, singing and comedy acts.

    "privateBeach": True or False, # Private beach. The beach which is in close proximity to the hotel is open only to guests.

    "scuba": True or False, # Scuba. Apparatus consists of a tank providing oxygen to the diver through a mask. Requires certification of the diver and supervision. The hotel may have the activity at its own waterfront or have an affiliation with a nearby facility. Required equipment is most often supplied to guests. Can be free or for a fee. Not snorkeling. Not done in a swimming pool.
    "scubaException": "A String", # Scuba exception.
    "snorkeling": True or False, # Snorkeling. The provision for guests to participate in a recreational water activity in which swimmers wear a diving mask, a simple, shaped breathing tube and flippers/swim fins for the purpose of exploring below the surface of an ocean, gulf or lake. Does not usually require user certification or professional supervision. Equipment may or may not be available for rent or purchase. Not scuba diving.
    "snorkelingException": "A String", # Snorkeling exception.
    "tennis": True or False, # Tennis. The hotel has the requisite court(s) on site or has an affiliation with a nearby facility for the purpose of providing guests with the opportunity to play a two-sided court-based game in which players use a stringed racquet to hit a ball across a net to the side of the opposing player. The court can be indoors or outdoors. Instructors, racquets and balls may or may not be provided.
    "tennisException": "A String", # Tennis exception.
    "waterSkiing": True or False, # Water skiing.     "waterSkiingException": "A String", # Water skiing exception.
    "watercraftRental": True or False, # Watercraft rental. The hotel owns water vessels that it permits guests to borrow and use. Can be free or for a fee. Watercraft may include boats, pedal boats, rowboats, sailboats, powerboats, canoes, kayaks, or personal watercraft (such as a Jet Ski).
    "watercraftRentalException": "A String", # Watercraft rental exception.

updateLodging(name, body=None, updateMask=None, x__xgafv=None) 
Updates the Lodging of a specific location.

Args:
  name: string, Required. Google identifier for this location in the form: `locations/{location_id}/lodging` (required)
  body: object, The request body.
    The object takes the form of:

{ # Lodging of a location that provides accomodations.
  "accessibility": { # Physical adaptations made to the property in consideration of varying levels of human physical ability. # Physical adaptations made to the property in consideration of varying levels of human physical ability.
    "mobilityAccessible": True or False, # Mobility accessible. Throughout the property there are physical adaptations to ease the stay of a person in a wheelchair, such as auto-opening doors, wide elevators, wide bathrooms or ramps.
    "mobilityAccessibleElevator": True or False, # Mobility accessible elevator. A lift that transports people from one level to another and is built to accommodate a wheelchair-using passenger owing to the width of its doors and placement of call buttons.
    "mobilityAccessibleElevatorException": "A String", # Mobility accessible elevator exception.
    "mobilityAccessibleException": "A String", # Mobility accessible exception.
    "mobilityAccessibleParking": True or False, # Mobility accessible parking. The presence of a marked, designated area of prescribed size in which only registered, labeled vehicles transporting a person with physical challenges may park.
    "mobilityAccessibleParkingException": "A String", # Mobility accessible parking exception.
    "mobilityAccessiblePool": True or False, # Mobility accessible pool. A swimming pool equipped with a mechanical chair that can be lowered and raised for the purpose of moving physically challenged guests into and out of the pool. May be powered by electricity or water. Also known as pool lift.
    "mobilityAccessiblePoolException": "A String", # Mobility accessible pool exception.
  },
